add_namespace = russia

#Navalny Admitted to Hospital
country_event = {
	id = russia.1
	title = russia.1.t
	desc = russia.1.d
	picture = GFX_Navalny
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = russia.1.a
		set_temp_variable = {
			var = SOV_election_approval_rating_nav_var_temp
			value = 0.025
		}
		SOV_add_election_approval_rating_nav = yes
	}
}

#Navalny Protests
country_event = {
	id = russia.2
	title = russia.2.t
	desc = russia.2.d
	picture = GFX_Navalny_Protests_Country
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = russia.2.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_navalny_protests_government_tooltip
		add_stability = -0.05
		news_event = { id = news.141 hours = 5 }
		set_temp_variable = {
			var = SOV_election_approval_rating_nav_var_temp
			value = 0.07
		}
		SOV_add_election_approval_rating_nav = yes
		set_temp_variable = {
			var = SOV_election_approval_rating_ur_var_temp
			value = -0.05
		}
		SOV_add_election_approval_rating_ur = yes	
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = SOV_navalny_protests_idea
			days = 365
		}
		
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = SOV_navalny_protests
			add_popularity = { 
				ideology = social_liberal
				popularity = 0.03
			}
			add_popularity = { 
				ideology = market_liberal
				popularity = 0.03
			}
		}	
	}
}

#Election Preparations
country_event = {
	id = russia.45
	title = russia.45.t
	desc = russia.45.d
	picture = GFX_SOV_presidential_elections
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { #cprf
		name = russia.45.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
			modifier = {
				factor = 10000
				has_game_rule = { rule = SOV_ai_behavior option = CPRF }
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_side_cprf
		custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_elections_started
		activate_mission = alliance_with_srzp_mission
		set_country_flag = SOV_sided_with_cprf_flag
		complete_national_focus = SOV_new_revolution
		hidden_effect = {
			activate_mission = SOV_countdown_day_mission
			activate_mission = SOV_opposition_growth_mission
			country_event = { id = russia.54 days = 30 }
			country_event = { id = russia.12 days = 50 }
			country_event = { id = russia.13 days = 20 }
			country_event = { id = russia.14 days = 70 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = SOV_ai_behavior option = CPRF }
					is_ai = yes
				}
				set_temp_variable = {
					var = SOV_election_approval_rating_cprf_var_temp
					value = 1
				}
				SOV_add_election_approval_rating_cprf = yes
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { #ldpr
		name = russia.45.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
			modifier = {
				factor = 10000
				has_game_rule = { rule = SOV_ai_behavior option = LDPR }
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_side_ldpr
		custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_elections_started
		set_country_flag = SOV_sided_with_ldpr_flag
		complete_national_focus = SOV_russian_destiny
		hidden_effect = {
			activate_mission = SOV_countdown_day_mission
			activate_mission = SOV_opposition_growth_mission
			country_event = { id = russia.53 days = 15 }
			country_event = { id = russia.54 days = 30 }
			country_event = { id = russia.12 days = 50 }
			country_event = { id = russia.13 days = 20 }
			country_event = { id = russia.14 days = 70 }
			if = {
				limit = { 
					has_game_rule = { rule = SOV_ai_behavior option = LDPR }
					is_ai = yes
				}
				set_temp_variable = {

country_event = {
	id = russia.101
	title = russia.101.t
	desc = russia.101.d
	picture = GFX_Generic_Oligarchs 
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {

	}
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = SOV_duma_category_disabled
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = russia.101.a #accept
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		unlock_decision_tooltip = { decision = SOV_invest_in_state_factory show_effect_tooltip = yes }
		event_target:SOV_oligarchs_investment_state = {
			set_state_flag = SOV_oligarchs_build_factory
			set_variable = { factory_goal = industrial_complex_level }
			add_to_variable = { factory_goal = 1 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = russia.101.b #refuse
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		ROOT = { clr_country_flag = SOV_oligarchs_investment }
		clear_global_event_target = SOV_oligarchs_investment_state
		set_temp_variable = {
			var = SOV_oligarch_approval_rating_var_temp
			value = -0.03
		}
		SOV_add_oligarch_approval_rating = yes
	}
}

# Oligarch wants investment in their state - hidden dispatch event
country_event = {
	id = russia.102
	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = SOV
		NOT = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = SOV_duma_category_disabled
				has_completed_focus = SOV_election_victory
				has_completed_focus = SOV_triumph_of_zhirinovsky
				has_completed_focus = SOV_russian_victory
				has_country_leader = {
					character = SOV_alexei_navalny
					ruling_only = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_country_flag = SOV_oligarchs_investment
		if = {
			limit = { has_event_target = SOV_oligarchs_investment_state }
			clear_global_event_target = SOV_oligarchs_investment_state
		}
		random_list = {
			60 = {
				modifier = {
					NOT = {
						any_owned_state = {
							is_core_of = ROOT
							is_controlled_by = ROOT
							free_building_slots = {
								building = industrial_complex
								size > 0
								include_locked = no
							}
						}
					}
					factor = 0
				}
				random_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						is_core_of = ROOT
						is_controlled_by = ROOT
						free_building_slots = {
							building = industrial_complex
							size > 0
							include_locked = no
						}
					}
					
					save_global_event_target_as = SOV_oligarchs_investment_state
					state_event = { id = russia.101 trigger_for = controller }
				}
			}
			40 = {
				modifier = {
					NOT = {
						any_owned_state = {
							is_core_of = ROOT
							is_controlled_by = ROOT
							free_building_slots = {
								building = arms_factory
								size > 0
								include_locked = no
							}
						}
					}
					factor = 0
				}
				modifier = {
					has_completed_focus = SOV_build_up_western_military_district_UR
					factor = 2
				}
				random_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						is_core_of = ROOT
						is_controlled_by = ROOT
						free_building_slots = {
							building = arms_factory
							size > 0
							include_locked = no
						}
					}
					save_global_event_target_as = SOV_oligarchs_investment_state
					state_event = { id = russia.103 trigger_for = controller }
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = russia.102 days = 365 random_days = 10 }
		}
	}
}

			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_completed_focus = SOV_election_victory }
					has_war = no
				}

			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_completed_focus = SOV_election_victory }
					OR = {
						has_war_with = UKR
						has_war_with = GER
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = russia.404 days = 180 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = russia.108.a
		army_experience = 10
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_war = yes
			}
			add_war_support = 0.03
		}

country_event = {
	id = russia.113
	title = russia.113.t
	desc = russia.113.d
	picture = GFX_Virgin_Commies
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = russia.113.a
		set_party_name = { ideology = totalitarian_socialist long_name = SOV_communist_totsoc_long name = SOV_communist_totsoc_short }
		set_party_name = { ideology = communist long_name = SOV_communist_authsoc_long name = SOV_communist_authsoc_short }
		set_party_name = { ideology = libertarian_socialist long_name = SOV_communist_libsoc_long name = SOV_communist_libsoc_short }
		set_party_name = { ideology = social_democrat long_name = SOV_communist_socdem_long name = SOV_communist_socdem_short }
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = libertarian_socialist
			}
			set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var_temp = token:social_democrat }
			add_to_coalition = yes
			set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var_temp = token:communist }
			add_to_coalition = yes
			set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var_temp = token:totalitarian_socialist }
			add_to_coalition = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = communist
			}
			set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var_temp = token:social_democrat }
			add_to_coalition = yes
			set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var_temp = token:libertarian_socialist }
			add_to_coalition = yes
			set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var_temp = token:totalitarian_socialist }
			add_to_coalition = yes
		}
		add_popularity = { 
			ideology = totalitarian_socialist
			popularity = 0.01
		}
		add_popularity = { 
			ideology = communist
			popularity = 0.01
		}
		add_popularity = { 
			ideology = libertarian_socialist
			popularity = 0.01
		}
		add_popularity = { 
			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = 0.01
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			retire_character = SOV_nikolay_rybakov
			retire_character = SOV_sergei_udaltsov
			retire_character = SOV_maxim_suraykin
			retire_character = SOV_sergei_naryshkin
			set_party_name = { ideology = nationalist long_name = SOV_union_nationalist_long name = SOV_union_nationalist_short }
			add_country_leader_role = {
			    character = SOV_valery_gerasimov
				promote_leader = yes
			    country_leader = {
			        ideology = military_junta
					expire="1.1.1.1"
					id=-1
			        traits = { }
			    }
			}
			promote_character = SOV_valery_gerasimov
			promote_character = SOV_pavel_grudinin
			promote_character = SOV_dmitry_novikov
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = communist
				}

			}
		}
	}
}

#Russian Army elements invade Kazakhstan
country_event = {
	id = russia.131
	title = russia.131.t
	desc = russia.131.d
	picture = GFX_South_Ossetian_Volunteers
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
	}
	option = {
		name = russia.131.a
		KAZ = {
			every_controlled_state = {
				add_core_of = KHI
				add_core_of = TAT
				add_core_of = KYR
				add_core_of = TAJ
				add_core_of = YAK
			}			
			remove_from_faction = KYR
		}

		UZB = {
			every_controlled_state = {
				add_core_of = KHI
				add_core_of = TAT
				add_core_of = KYR
				add_core_of = TAJ
				add_core_of = YAK
			}			
		}

		KYR = {
			every_controlled_state = {

	}
}

#Terrorists in Western Ukraine and Baltics
country_event = {
	id = russia.228
	title = russia.228.t
	desc = russia.228.d
	picture = GFX_Generic_SOBR
	
	is_triggered_only = yes	
	immediate = {
	hidden_effect = {
		#Ukraine
		if = {
			limit = { UKR = { exists = no } }
			73 = {
				remove_core_of = SOV
				add_resistance = 30
			}
			89 = {
				remove_core_of = SOV
				add_resistance = 60
			}
			91 = {
				remove_core_of = SOV
				add_resistance = 40
			}
			93 = {
				remove_core_of = SOV
				add_resistance = 30
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { EST = { exists = no } }
			every_controlled_state = {
				if = {
					limit = { is_core_of = EST }
					remove_core_of = SOV
					add_resistance = 40
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { LAT = { exists = no } }
			every_controlled_state = {
				if = {
					limit = { is_core_of = LAT }
					remove_core_of = SOV
					add_resistance = 40
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { LIT = { exists = no } }
			every_controlled_state = {
				if = {
					limit = { is_core_of = LIT }
					remove_core_of = SOV
					add_resistance = 40
				}
			}
		}
	}
	}
	option = {
		name = russia.228.a
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = SOV_soviet_cto
		}
		unlock_decision_category_tooltip = SOV_western_states_terrorists_category
		add_political_power = 100
		set_temp_variable = {
			var = society_development_var_temp
			value = -0.10
		}
		add_society_development = yes
		set_temp_variable = {
			var = industrial_development_var_temp
			value = -0.10
		}
		add_industrial_development = yes
	}
}

#Negotiations with the opposition are successful!
country_event = {
	id = russia.229
	title = russia.229.t
	desc = russia.229.d
	picture = GFX_Generic_SOBR
	
	is_triggered_only = yes	
	immediate = {
	}
	option = {
		name = russia.229.a
		hidden_effect = {
		if = {
				limit = { UKR = { exists = no } }
				73 = {
					add_resistance = -10
					add_compliance = 25
				}
				89 = {
					add_resistance = -10
					add_compliance = 25
				}
				91 = {
					add_resistance = -10
					add_compliance = 25
				}
				93 = {
					add_resistance = -10
					add_compliance = 25
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { EST = { exists = no } }
				every_controlled_state = {
					if = {
						limit = { is_core_of = EST }
						add_resistance = -10
						add_compliance = 25
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { LAT = { exists = no } }
				every_controlled_state = {
					if = {
						limit = { is_core_of = LAT }
						add_resistance = -10
						add_compliance = 25
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { LIT = { exists = no } }
				every_controlled_state = {
					if = {
						limit = { is_core_of = LIT }
						add_resistance = -10
						add_compliance = 25
					}
				}
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_negotiations_successful_tooltip
	}
}

#Negotiations with the opposition are not successful!
country_event = {
	id = russia.230
	title = russia.230.t
	desc = russia.230.d
	picture = GFX_Generic_SOBR
	
	is_triggered_only = yes	
	immediate = {
	}
	option = {
		name = russia.230.a
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { UKR = { exists = no } }
				73 = {
					add_resistance = 25
					add_compliance = -10
				}
				89 = {
					add_resistance = 25
					add_compliance = -10
				}
				91 = {
					add_resistance = 25
					add_compliance = -10
				}
				93 = {
					add_resistance = 25
					add_compliance = -10
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { EST = { exists = no } }
				every_controlled_state = {
					if = {
						limit = { is_core_of = EST }
						add_resistance = 25
						add_compliance = -10
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { LAT = { exists = no } }
				every_controlled_state = {
					if = {
						limit = { is_core_of = LAT }
						add_resistance = 25
						add_compliance = -10
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { LIT = { exists = no } }
				every_controlled_state = {
					if = {
						limit = { is_core_of = LIT }
						add_resistance = 25
						add_compliance = -10
					}
				}
			}
			add_stability = -0.05
			add_political_power = -25
			custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_negotiations_unsuccessful_tooltip
		}
	}
}

				}

					type = arms_factory
					damage = 1
				}
			}
		}

					damage = 1
				}

				}
			}

	}

#I'm a fucking collaborator
country_event = {
	id = russia.237
	title = russia.237.t
	desc = russia.237.d
	picture = GFX_Tula_Attack  
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = HUN
			}
			set_politics = {	
				ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			set_popularities = {
				conservative = 17
				social_democrat = 15
				authoritarian_democrat = 37
				market_liberal = 8
				nationalist = 4
				communist = 19
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = HUN_Tibor_Benko_char
				picture = "gfx/Leaders/HUN/Portrait_Tibor_Benko.png"
				ideology = military_democracy
			}
			set_party_name = { ideology = authoritarian_democrat long_name = HUN_collaborationist_long name = HUN_collaborationist_short }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = SLO
			}
			set_politics = {	
				ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			set_popularities = {
				fascist = 8
				conservative = 16
				market_liberal = 4
				authoritarian_democrat = 38
				social_democrat = 9
				communist = 23
				social_liberal = 2
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = SLO_Daniel_Zmeko
				picture = "gfx/Leaders/SLO/Daniel_Zmeko.png"
				ideology = military_democracy
			}
			set_party_name = { ideology = authoritarian_democrat long_name = SLO_collaborationist_long name = SLO_collaborationist_short }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = ROM
			}
			set_politics = {	
				ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			set_popularities = {
				conservative = 	11
				market_liberal = 12
				social_liberal = 5
				authoritarian_democrat = 33
				social_democrat = 6
				libertarian_socialist = 24
				social_liberal = 9
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = ROM_Vasile_Dynku_char
				picture = "gfx/Leaders/ROM/Vasile_Dynku.png"
				ideology = hybrid_regime
			}
			set_party_name = { ideology = authoritarian_democrat long_name = ROM_collaborationist_long name = ROM_collaborationist_short }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = BUL
			}
			set_politics = {	
				ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			set_popularities = {
				conservative = 	10
				market_liberal = 6
				social_liberal = 5
				authoritarian_democrat = 35
				social_democrat = 10
				communist = 25
				social_liberal = 9
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = BUL_rumen_radev_char
				picture = "gfx/Leaders/BUL/Rumen Radev.png"
				ideology = hybrid_regime
			}
			set_party_name = { ideology = authoritarian_democrat long_name = BUL_collaborationist_long name = BUL_collaborationist_short }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = russia.237.a
	}
}

		}

#Looting the Steel Crown
country_event = {
	id = russia.245
	title = russia.245.t
	desc = russia.245.d
	picture = GFX_Steel_Crown
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
	}
	
	option = {
		name = russia.245.a
		add_political_power = -5
			random_country_division = {
				limit = {	
					division_has_battalion_in_template = mot_militia
					division_has_battalion_in_template = mechanized
					division_has_battalion_in_template = modern_armor
					is_unit_template_reserves = no
				}
				add_history_entry = {
					key = "Partook in the looting of the Steel Crown of Carol I."
					subject = "Division Honor"
					allow = yes
				}									
			}		
	}
}

#Soviet Election 2
country_event = {
	id = russia.247
	title = russia.247.t
	desc = russia.247.d
	picture = GFX_APLA_Congress
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = SOV_open_diplo_tree
			set_country_flag = SOV_open_econ_tree
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Parfenov
		name = russia.247.a
		trigger = {
			#has_country_flag = SOV_united_candidate
			always = no
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = libertarian_socialist
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				retire_ideology_leader = libertarian_socialist
				promote_character = {
					character = SOV_denis_parfenov
					ideology = eurocommunism
				}
			}
		
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = libertarian_socialist
				popularity = 0.1
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = libertarian_socialist
				elections_allowed = yes
				#last_election = "[GetDateStringNoHour]"
    			election_frequency = 48
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = communist
				NOT = {
					has_completed_focus = SOV_class_unity
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				retire_ideology_leader = communist
				promote_character = {
					character = SOV_denis_parfenov
					ideology = marxism_leninism
				}
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = communist
				popularity = 0.1
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = communist
				elections_allowed = yes
				#last_election = "[GetDateStringNoHour]"
    			election_frequency = 48
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				has_government = communist
				has_completed_focus = SOV_class_unity
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				retire_ideology_leader = communist
				promote_character = {
					character = SOV_denis_parfenov
					ideology = market_socialism
				}
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = communist
				popularity = 0.1
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = communist
				elections_allowed = yes
				#last_election = "[GetDateStringNoHour]"
    			election_frequency = 48
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				has_government = communist
				has_country_leader_ideology = left_nationalism
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				retire_ideology_leader = communist
				promote_character = {
					character = SOV_denis_parfenov
					ideology = left_nationalism
				}
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = communist
				popularity = 0.1
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = communist
				elections_allowed = yes
				#last_election = "[GetDateStringNoHour]"
    			election_frequency = 48
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #Soviet Lukashenko
		name = russia.247.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = SOV_united_candidate }
			has_government = communist
			is_power_balance_in_range = {
				id = SOV_communist_party_balance
				range > SOV_old_guard_dominant_range
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			retire_ideology_leader = communist
			promote_character = {
				character = SOV_aleksandr_lukashenko
				ideology = left_nationalism
			}
			clr_country_flag = head_of_gov_ui_enabled
		}
		set_country_flag = SOV_lukashenko_elected
		mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
		complete_national_focus = SOV_new_lukashenko_era
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = communist
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = communist
			elections_allowed = yes
			#last_election = "[GetDateStringNoHour]"
    		election_frequency = 48
		}
	}
	option = { #Levchenko
		name = russia.247.c
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = SOV_united_candidate }
			has_government = libertarian_socialist
			is_power_balance_in_range = {
				id = SOV_communist_party_balance
				range < SOV_new_guard_dominant_range
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			retire_ideology_leader = libertarian_socialist
			promote_character = SOV_sergey_levchenko
		}
		set_country_flag = SOV_levchenko_elected
		mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
		complete_national_focus = SOV_protege
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = libertarian_socialist
			popularity = 0.1
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = libertarian_socialist
			elections_allowed = yes
			#last_election = "[GetDateStringNoHour]"
    		election_frequency = 48
		}
		add_country_leader_trait = hos_capital_p_president
	}
	option = {
		name = russia.247.e #Afonin
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = SOV_united_candidate }
			has_government = communist
			is_power_balance_in_range = {
				id = SOV_communist_party_balance
				range < SOV_old_guard_power_range
			}
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = communist
			elections_allowed = yes

country_event = {
	id = russia.3
	title = russia.324.t
	desc = russia.324.d
	picture = GFX_generic_lenin
	 
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
	    hidden_effect = {
			
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = russia.324.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = SOV_ADS_member_flag }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				tag = KAZ
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				tag = ARM
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 100
				tag = MON
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 100
				tag = SWZ
			}
		}
		SOV_join_ADS = yes
		if = {
			limit = { 
				OR = {
					original_tag = CHL
					original_tag = BRA
					original_tag = BOL
					original_tag = COL
				}
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = libertarian_socialist
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = libertarian_socialist
				popularity = 0.2
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				original_tag = MON
			}
			country_event = {
				id = russia.127
				days = 30
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				OR = {
					original_tag = PRU
					original_tag = ANG
					original_tag = MZB
					original_tag = SWZ
					original_tag = ERI
					original_tag = ZIM
				}
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = communist
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = communist
				popularity = 0.2
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = social_democrat
				popularity = -0.2
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = libertarian_socialist
				popularity = -0.2
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					original_tag = ERI
				}
				set_country_leader_ideology = marxism_leninism
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = russia.324.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 3
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_government = totalitarian_socialist
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_government = communist
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_government = libertarian_socialist
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_government = social_democrat
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				tag = AZR
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				tag = TAJ
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				tag = UZB
			}
		}
	}
}

	fire_only_once = yes

	    name = russia.387.a
		add_political_power = -100
		add_power_balance_value = {
			id = SOV_LDPR_balance
			value = -0.05
		}
		add_popularity = {
		    ideology = authoritarian_democrat
			popularity = 0.05
		}	
		add_popularity = {
		    ideology = communist
			popularity = 0.02
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
			    has_idea = SOV_KNOA_idea
				}
			swap_ideas = {
			    remove_idea = SOV_KNOA_idea
                add_idea = SOV_KNOA_2_idea
			}
		}
		else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = SOV_KNOA_2_idea
			    }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = SOV_KNOA_2_idea
                    add_idea = SOV_KNOA_3_idea
				}
		    }
		else_if = {
			remove_ideas = SOV_KNOA_3_idea
		}
		set_country_flag = SOV_ldpr_pardon_left_patriots
		hidden_effect = {
		    country_event = { id = russia.388 days = 150 random_days = 20 }
		}
	}
	option = { #KILL THEM, DOESNT MATTER PI CONSIDERS CPRF FAKE SOCDEM REVISIONISTS
	    name = russia.387.b
		add_war_support = 0.05
		add_power_balance_value = {

		}

		    ideology = fascist
			popularity = 0.05
		}

		}
	}

			}

				leave_faction = yes

		}

			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {

				}

#Zyuganov ustal
country_event = {
	id = russia.453
	title = russia.453.t
	desc = russia.453.d
	picture = GFX_SOV_House
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = SOV_zyuganov_retired
			clr_country_flag = head_of_gov_ui_enabled
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = SOV_Zyuganov
				}
				remove_ideas = SOV_Zyuganov
				add_ideas = vacant_hog
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_character = SOV_gennady_zyuganov
				}
				retire_character = SOV_gennady_zyuganov
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = russia.453.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = SOV_Zyuganov
				}
				remove_ideas = SOV_Zyuganov
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_character = SOV_gennady_zyuganov
				}
				retire_character = SOV_gennady_zyuganov
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = russia.473
	title = {
		text = russia.473.t1
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				NOT = { has_completed_focus = SOV_recognize_donbas }
				NOT =  { has_completed_focus = SOV_the_time_is_now }
			}
		}
	}
	title = {
		text = russia.473.t2
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_completed_focus = SOV_recognize_donbas
				has_completed_focus = SOV_the_time_is_now
			}
		}
	}
	desc = russia.473.d
	picture = GFX_SOV_donbas_3
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = SOV_novorossiya_formed_flag
			NOV = {
				add_ideas = {
					NOV_united_novorossiya_idea
					NOV_donbas_economy_idea
					NOV_army_of_novorossiya_idea
				}
			}
			news_event = { id = news.320 hours = 6 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = russia.473.a
		NOV = {
			add_ideas = {
				NOV_united_novorossiya_idea
				NOV_donbas_economy_idea
				NOV_army_of_novorossiya_idea
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_completed_focus = SOV_recognize_donbas }
			add_political_power = -100
		}		
		if = {
			limit = { has_completed_focus = SOV_the_time_is_now }
			add_political_power = -100
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			NOV = {
				remove_ideas = NOV_lugansk_economy_idea
				remove_ideas = NOV_lugansk_reform_frenzy_idea
				remove_ideas = NOV_peoples_militia_idea
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_completed_focus = SOV_recognize_donbas }
				NOV = {
					set_cosmetic_tag = NOV_unified
					set_party_name = {
						ideology = authoritarian_democrat
						long_name = NOV_authdem_united_party
						name = NOV_authdem_united_party
					}
					promote_character = {
						character = NOV_denis_pushilin
						ideology = hybrid_regime
					}
					set_country_leader_ideology = ultra_conservatism
				}
				NOV = {
					annex_country = {
						target = DPR
						transfer_troops = yes
					}
					set_capital = {
						state = 227
						remember_old_capital = yes
					}
				}
				227 = {
					add_core_of = NOV
				}		
				1374 = {
					add_core_of = NOV
				}		
				1091 = {
					add_core_of = NOV
				}	
				227 = {
					remove_core_of = DPR
				}
				1374 = {
					remove_core_of = DPR
				}		
				1091 = {
					remove_core_of = DPR
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_completed_focus = SOV_the_time_is_now }
				NOV = {
					set_cosmetic_tag = NOV_zhir
					set_party_name = {
						ideology = fascist
						long_name = NOV_fascist_ldpr_party
						name = NOV_fascist_ldpr_party_short
					}
					promote_character = {
						character = NOV_denis_pushilin_nationalist
						ideology = classical_fascism
					}
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = fascist
						elections_allowed = no
					}
				}
				NOV = {
					annex_country = {
						target = DPR
						transfer_troops = yes
					}
					set_capital = {
						state = 227
						remember_old_capital = yes
					}
				}
				227 = {
					add_core_of = NOV
				}		
				1374 = {
					add_core_of = NOV
				}		
				1091 = {
					add_core_of = NOV
				}

	desc = russia.477.d

	}

		name = russia.477.a
		add_political_power = -25
		add_war_support = -0.05

			var = SOV_election_approval_rating_ldpr_var_temp
			value = 0.015
		}
		SOV_add_election_approval_rating_ldpr = yes		
	}
}

#Assassination Attempt on Putin
country_event = {
	id = russia.487
	title = russia.487.t
	desc = russia.487.d
	picture = GFX_SOV_Assassination_Attempt
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		SOV = {
			has_country_leader = {
				character = SOV_vladimir_putin
				ruling_only = yes
			}
		}
		NOT = { has_country_flag = SOV_putin_ill_more_flag }
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = russia.488 days = 5 }
			set_portraits = {
				character = SOV_vladimir_putin
				civilian = { large ="GFX_portrait_SOV_vladimir_putin_post_assassination" }
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #a close call!
		name = russia.487.a
		set_country_flag = SOV_assassination_attempt_happened_flag
		add_stability = -0.1
		add_political_power = -100
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = russia.490 days = 8 }
		}
	}
}

				has_country_flag = SOV_infiltrated_CPRF2
				has_country_flag = SOV_infiltrated_CPRF 
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
	}
	
	option = { #shitters
		name = russia.492.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = SOV_push_back_the_west
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_centralize_power_focus_needed_tt
		}		
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = SOV_putinism_with_human_face
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_reform_power_focus_needed_tt
		}
		add_political_power = -10
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = communist
			popularity = 0.01
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = russia.492 days = 60 random_days = 10 }
		}
	}
}

#Another War Bond
country_event = {
	id = russia.497
	title = russia.497.t
	desc = russia.497.d
	picture = GFX_Rodina_party
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
	}
	immediate = {
		
	}
	
	option = {
		name = russia.497.a
		set_temp_variable = {
			var = war_bond
			value = SOV.max_manpower_k
		}
		multiply_temp_variable = { war_bond = 0.3 }
		multiply_temp_variable = { war_bond = SOV.has_war_support }
		multiply_temp_variable = { war_bond = SOV.party_popularity@ruling_party }
		divide_temp_variable = { war_bond = 10000 }
		set_temp_variable = {
			var = income_var_temp
			value = war_bond
		}
		add_income = yes
		set_temp_variable = {
			var = war_bond_2
			value = war_bond
		}
		set_temp_variable_to_random = {
			var = random_temp_var
			min = 70
			max = 100
			integer = yes
		}
		multiply_temp_variable = { war_bond_2 = random_temp_var }
		round_temp_variable = war_bond_2
		add_cic = war_bond_2
		set_temp_variable = {
			var = war_bond_3
			value = war_bond
		}
		multiply_temp_variable = { war_bond_3 = 20 }
		round_temp_variable = war_bond_3
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = SOV_ruble_for_fuhrer
			}
			modify_timed_idea = {
				idea = SOV_ruble_for_fuhrer
				days = war_bond_3
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = SOV_ruble_for_fuhrer
				days = war_bond_3
			}
		}
	}
}

		multiply_temp_variable = { volunteers_var = SOV.party_popularity@ruling_party }

		add_manpower = volunteers_var
		add_political_power = 25
	}
}
#War charity
country_event = {
	id = russia.499
	title = russia.499.t
	desc = russia.499.d
	picture = GFX_SOV_war_charity
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
	}
	immediate = {
		
	}
	
	option = {
		name = russia.499.a
		set_temp_variable = {
			var = support_var
			value = SOV.max_manpower_k
		}
		multiply_temp_variable = { support_var = SOV.has_war_support }
		multiply_temp_variable = { support_var = SOV.party_popularity@ruling_party }
		divide_temp_variable = { support_var = 450 }
		round_temp_variable = support_var
		set_temp_variable = {
			var = bpla_var
			value = support_var
		}
		set_temp_variable_to_random = {
			var = random_temp_var
			min = 0.3
			max = 0.6
		}
		multiply_temp_variable = { bpla_var = random_temp_var }
		round_temp_variable = bpla_var
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
			type = support_equipment
			amount = support_var
			producer = SOV
		}
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
			type = guided_missile_equipment_1
			amount = bpla_var
			producer = SOV
		}
	}
}
#International ADS Help
country_event = {
	id = russia.500
	title = russia.500.t
	desc = russia.500.d
	picture = GFX_SOV_war_help
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
	}
	immediate = {
		
	}
	
	option = {
		name = russia.500.a
		set_temp_variable = { rifles_var = random }
		set_temp_variable = { artillery_var = random }
		set_temp_variable = { btr_var = random }
		set_temp_variable = { bmp_var = random }
		set_temp_variable = { fuel_var = random }
		multiply_temp_variable = { rifles_var = SOV_ADS_number_of_members }
		multiply_temp_variable = { artillery_var = SOV_ADS_number_of_members }
		multiply_temp_variable = { btr_var = SOV_ADS_number_of_members }
		multiply_temp_variable = { bmp_var = SOV_ADS_number_of_members }
		multiply_temp_variable = { fuel_var = SOV_ADS_number_of_members }
		multiply_temp_variable = { rifles_var = 70 }
		multiply_temp_variable = { fuel_var = 70 }
		multiply_temp_variable = { artillery_var = 7 }
		multiply_temp_variable = { btr_var = 7 }
		multiply_temp_variable = { bmp_var = 7 }
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
			type = infantry_equipment_1
			amount = rifles_var
		}
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
			type = spaa_equipment
			amount = artillery_var
		}
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
			type = mechanized_equipment
			amount = btr_var
		}
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
			type = light_mechanized_equipment
			amount = bmp_var
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				fuel_ratio > 0.5
			}
			add_fuel = fuel_var
		}
	}
}

			limit = {
				has_government = libertarian_socialist
			}
			add_popularity = { 
				ideology = libertarian_socialist
				popularity = -0.03
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = communist
			}
			add_popularity = { 
				ideology = communist
				popularity = -0.03
			}
		}
		add_popularity = { 
			ideology = fascist
			popularity = 0.03
		}
		add_ideas = SOV_anti_soviet_resistanse_1
		unlock_decision_tooltip = SOV_utilize_antifa
		unlock_decision_tooltip = SOV_utilize_nazbol

		set_variable = {
			var = SOV_utilize_antifa_variable
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			var = SOV_utilize_nazbol_variable
			value = 0
		}

			}
			set_party_name = { 
				ideology = fascist
				long_name = SOV_fascist_nrg_long
				name = SOV_fascist_nrg_short
			}		
		}
	}

		remove_from_coalition = yes
		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var_temp = token:totalitarian_socialist }
		remove_from_coalition = yes
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = communist
			popularity = 0.02
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = totalitarian_socialist
			popularity = 0.02
		}
		add_stability = -0.05
		set_temp_variable = {
			var = society_development_var_temp
			value = -0.1
		}
		add_society_development = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			set_party_name = { ideology = totalitarian_socialist long_name = SOV_union_united_long name = SOV_union_united_short }

#Choosing new marshal
country_event = {
	id = russia.546
	title = russia.546.t
	desc = russia.546.d
	picture = GFX_SOV_military_parade_generals
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
	}
	
	immediate = {
	}
	
	option = { #Gerasimov
		name = russia.546.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_government = communist
					has_government = libertarian_socialist
				}
			}
			add_trait = {
				character = SOV_valery_gerasimov
				slot = field_marshal
				trait = trait_SOV_marshal_of_soviet_union
			}
		}	
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_government = fascist
				}
			}
			add_trait = {
				character = SOV_valery_gerasimov
				slot = field_marshal
				trait = trait_SOV_marshal_of_russia
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_trait = {
				character = SOV_valery_gerasimov
				slot = field_marshal
				trait = trait_SOV_marshal_of_russian_federation
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #Salyukov
		name = russia.546.b
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_government = communist
					has_government = libertarian_socialist
				}
			}
			add_trait = {
				character = SOV_oleg_salyukov
				slot = field_marshal
				trait = trait_SOV_marshal_of_soviet_union
			}
		}		
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_government = fascist
				}
			}
			add_trait = {
				character = SOV_oleg_salyukov
				slot = field_marshal
				trait = trait_SOV_marshal_of_russia
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_trait = {
				character = SOV_oleg_salyukov
				slot = field_marshal
				trait = trait_SOV_marshal_of_russian_federation
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #Gulevich Union State
		name = russia.546.c
		trigger = {
			BLR = {
				exists = no
			}
			SOV = {
				has_government = authoritarian_democrat
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -25
		add_trait = {
			character = BLR_viktor_gulevich
			slot = field_marshal
			trait = trait_SOV_marshal_of_union_state
		}
	}
}

		every_controlled_state = {
			random_select_amount  = 5
			add_dynamic_modifier = { 
				modifier = SOV_regional_rightist_administartion
			}
		}
		every_controlled_state = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = SOV_regional_rightist_administartion
					has_dynamic_modifier = SOV_regional_liberal_administartion
				}
			}
			random_select_amount  = 5
			add_dynamic_modifier = {
				modifier = SOV_regional_leftist_administartion
			}
		}		
		every_controlled_state = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = SOV_regional_rightist_administartion
					has_dynamic_modifier = SOV_regional_leftist_administartion
				}
			}
			random_select_amount  = 2
			add_dynamic_modifier = {
				modifier = SOV_regional_liberal_administartion
			}
		}
	}
}

# Oligarch wants investment in their state - hidden dispatch event
country_event = {
	id = russia.623
	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = SOV
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = SOV_nav_oligarch_subdued_flag
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_country_flag = SOV_oligarchs_investment
		if = {
			limit = { has_event_target = SOV_oligarchs_investment_state }
			clear_global_event_target = SOV_oligarchs_investment_state
		}
		random_list = {
			60 = {
				modifier = {
					NOT = {
						any_owned_state = {
							is_core_of = ROOT
							is_controlled_by = ROOT
							free_building_slots = {
								building = industrial_complex
								size > 0
								include_locked = no
							}
						}
					}
					factor = 0
				}
				random_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						is_core_of = ROOT
						is_controlled_by = ROOT
						free_building_slots = {
							building = industrial_complex
							size > 0
							include_locked = no
						}
					}
					
					save_global_event_target_as = SOV_oligarchs_investment_state
					state_event = { id = russia.622 trigger_for = controller }
				}
			}
			40 = {
				modifier = {
					NOT = {
						any_owned_state = {
							is_core_of = ROOT
							is_controlled_by = ROOT
							free_building_slots = {
								building = arms_factory
								size > 0
								include_locked = no
							}
						}
					}
					factor = 0
				}
				modifier = {
					has_completed_focus = SOV_build_up_western_military_district_UR
					factor = 2
				}
				random_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						is_core_of = ROOT
						is_controlled_by = ROOT
						free_building_slots = {
							building = arms_factory
							size > 0
							include_locked = no
						}
					}
					save_global_event_target_as = SOV_oligarchs_investment_state
					state_event = { id = russia.624 trigger_for = controller }
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = russia.623 days = 365 random_days = 10 }
		}
	}
}

	title = russia.700.t
	desc = russia.700.d
	picture = GFX_Generic_Grudinin
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
	}
	
	option = {
		name = russia.700.a
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_democrat
			elections_allowed = yes
			election_frequency = 48
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = 0.25
		}
		set_country_flag = SOV_grudinin_coup
		remove_power_balance = {
			id = SOV_communist_party_balance
		}
		focus_unlock = yes
		complete_national_focus = SOV_leader_russia_needs
		hidden_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var_temp = token:communist }
			add_to_coalition = yes
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = communist
				popularity = -0.1
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = conservative
				popularity = -0.05
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = totalitarian_socialist
				popularity = -0.05
			}
		}
	}
}

				long_name = SOV_lukashenko_apf_nationalists_long
				name = SOV_lukashenko_apf_nationalists_short
			}	
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = fascist
				long_name = SOV_lukashenko_apf_nationalists_long
				name = SOV_lukashenko_apf_nationalists_short
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = SOV_infiltrate_right_opposition_flag
				}
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = totalitarian_socialist
					long_name = SOV_lukashenko_apf_national_patriots_long
					name = SOV_lukashenko_apf_national_patriots_short
				}
				set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var_temp = token:national_socialist }
				add_to_coalition = yes

#International BRICS Help
country_event = {
	id = russia.729
	title = russia.729.t
	desc = russia.729.d
	picture = GFX_SOV_war_help
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
	}
	immediate = {
		
	}
	
	option = {
		name = russia.729.a
		set_temp_variable = { rifles_var = random }
		set_temp_variable = { artillery_var = random }
		set_temp_variable = { btr_var = random }
		set_temp_variable = { bmp_var = random }
		set_temp_variable = { fuel_var = random }
		multiply_temp_variable = { rifles_var = SOV_brics_number_of_members }
		multiply_temp_variable = { artillery_var = SOV_brics_number_of_members }
		multiply_temp_variable = { btr_var = SOV_brics_number_of_members }
		multiply_temp_variable = { bmp_var = SOV_brics_number_of_members }
		multiply_temp_variable = { fuel_var = SOV_brics_number_of_members }
		multiply_temp_variable = { rifles_var = 70 }
		multiply_temp_variable = { fuel_var = 70 }
		multiply_temp_variable = { artillery_var = 7 }
		multiply_temp_variable = { btr_var = 7 }
		multiply_temp_variable = { bmp_var = 7 }
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
			type = infantry_equipment_1
			amount = rifles_var
		}
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
			type = spaa_equipment
			amount = artillery_var
		}
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
			type = mechanized_equipment
			amount = btr_var
		}
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
			type = light_mechanized_equipment
			amount = bmp_var
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				fuel_ratio > 0.5
			}
			add_fuel = fuel_var
		}
	}
}

			}
		}
		SOV_join_brics = yes
		add_ideas = SOV_russo_finish_partnership_idea
		SOV = {
			country_event = { id = russia.731 hours = 1 }
		}
	}

		name = russia.730.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25

				factor = 50
				NOT = { has_government = authoritarian_democrat }
			}
		}
		SOV = {
			country_event = { id = russia.732 hours = 1 }
		}
	}
}

			set_party_name = { ideology = social_liberal long_name = SOV_medvedev_social_liberal_party_long name = SOV_medvedev_social_liberal_party_short }

			remove_ideas = SOV_neo_putinism
